World Snippets 111

— Sea Guest

▲ In the London Zoo, there is a wolf that can shake hands and bow to visitors, an Australian wild dog that can play with its keeper, and a five-year-old fox that can hold a milk bottle and drink milk.

▲ Twenty years ago, the British Consulate-General in Buenos Aires, the capital of Argentina in South America, was located in the back room of a shoe repair shop. Its simplicity is laughable.

▲ The United States uses no less than six million pairs of socks made of rayon every year. This silk is made from wood pulp and chemicals.

▲ The Danube River in Europe is one of the world's great rivers, measuring 2,000 miles long. The number of dialects spoken in the areas it flows through is as many as fifty-two.

▲ According to a British naturalist, a caterpillar (referring to those that transform into butterflies or moths when fully grown) consumes six thousand times its own weight in one month. If we compare this to a human male and use his weight as a ratio, it would take him three months to finish eating.

▲ Britain has invented a new type of balloon specifically for lifting sunken ships. Its construction is similar to ordinary balloons.

▲ Although Spain is rich in mineral resources, its industries are relatively small compared to other countries. Even in terms of railroads, it only has over 10,000 miles.

▲ Whale sharks in the Indian and Pacific Oceans often reach a length of sixty feet, but they pose no threat to humans.

Minor Tales of the "Da Ji" Ship Disaster 112

— Zhonghuan

The "Da Ji" wheel steamer of the Da Da Shipping Company runs the Shanghai-Yangzhou route, passing through Nantong, Rugao, Jiangyin, Jingjiang, Taixing, and other ports before reaching Yangzhou. On the evening of the 10th of this month [March], the ship left Shanghai as usual, carrying about 500 passengers and cargo including eighty boxes of sulfur, sugar paper, and other items. The next afternoon (the 11th), it passed Tiansheng Port in Nantong, where nearly 200 people disembarked. Several dozen anti-smuggling soldiers from that port boarded the ship to go to Yangzhou. The soldiers were smoking and having fun on the ship. By this time, the ship had passed the newly risen Zhang and Huang ports in Rugao and was heading towards Jiangyin. But joy turned to sorrow, and a tragic disaster erupted. When the ship caught fire, the crew panicked.

Approximately two hundred people lost their lives. Various reports have been published in the newspapers. Without assigning blame for the disaster, here are some minor tales:

▲ The Shi Family Donates Coffins Although the Da Da steamer has been running the Shanghai-Yangzhou route for many years, it has not set up docks in ports other than Shanghai and Tiansheng Port. Passengers are ferried back and forth by rowboats. On this day, a Mrs. Shi from Shanghai was returning to her hometown on the ship. She boarded a rowboat prepared by the Zhanghuang Port branch office to go ashore (about three miles from the shore). As the rowboat was about to reach the shore, a huge explosion was heard from the river. It was thought that the Da Ji's boiler had exploded. Mrs. Shi later received confirmation that the Da Ji had caught fire and many people had died. The Shi family is wealthy. If the disaster had occurred an hour earlier, their lives would not have been saved. Therefore, they generously donated several coffins for collecting bodies.

▲ Father Dies, Son Sacrificed Shizhuang Town, located a few miles from Xin Sheng Port, is a bustling market. During this New Year period, various shops usually go to other ports to purchase goods. On this day, Mr. Yu Youji, Mingxun, and the Shen brothers traveled from Xin Sheng Port to Jiangyin on the ship to purchase goods. There has been no news of them to date. Mr. Shen's wife is pregnant. Upon hearing the news, she cried bitterly, wishing she were dead. As a result of this shock, she had a miscarriage. It can truly be said that the father died and the son was sacrificed.

▲ Dying Together Mr. A, who was working in Shanghai, took the ship home with his wife, parents, and son, a total of five people. During the fire, they jumped into the river one after another. The husband was rescued by another ship, but when he looked around, he could not find any of his family members. Realizing that life had no meaning, he jumped into the river to commit suicide. It was truly tragic.

▲ Superstitious Rumors Three years ago, the Xin Da Ming steamer of the Da Tong Shipping Company, which also ran the Shanghai-Yangzhou route, was not far from the Kou'an Town dock in Taixing when it was rammed by the Japanese imperialist Atsuta Maru. The Da Ji heard the news in the rear and rushed to the rescue. When the Xin Da Ming saw the Da Ji approaching, it used an iron cable to tie itself to the right side of the Da Ji. Passengers on the Xin Da Ming rushed to the left side in order to jump into the Da Ji and escape. At that critical moment, the passengers gathered on one side, causing the Xin Da Ming to list to the left. The Da Ji was almost sunk, so the iron cable was cut. The Xin Da Ming immediately sank to the bottom of the river, killing about 200 people. According to superstitious people, the Xin Da Ming was not saved because the Da Ji cut the cable. Since then, the Da Ji would vaguely see the Xin Da Ming following behind. Today, the Da Ji sank because the Xin Da Ming was causing trouble. This is unfounded talk and laughable.

Talking About Unusual Bamboos 113

— Zheng Yimei

Bamboo has long been praised as a fine object for its humble heart. Therefore, the Six Recluses of Zhuxi and the Seven Sages of the Bamboo Grove, all outstanding figures of ancient times, were naturally in harmony with this gentleman [bamboo]. A knowledgeable guest spoke of the unusual types of bamboo, saying that Tengzhou in Shandong Province produces square bamboo, which is strong enough to be used as a cane. Mount Tiantai also produces bamboo that is square, green, and dripping with moisture, even better than that produced in Tengzhou. Junshan Mountain in Yueyang, Hunan Province also produces square bamboo, but it is soft and long, and not suitable for making materials. Chen Ding's Bamboo Genealogy has described this. A certain mountain in Fujian Province produces red bamboo. The young bamboo is yellow, and turns dark red as it gets older. The branches and leaves also change color with the bamboo. When looking from afar at the cluster of bamboos on the hillside, it is like a forest of maple trees covered with frost. A wealthy family spent a huge sum of money to purchase red bamboo for their garden and built a red bamboo building to show off their elegance, reminiscent of Wang Yucheng's Yellow Hill Bamboo Tower. On the day of its completion, they held a grand banquet for guests, enjoying the pleasures of singing and poetry. A famous scholar wrote a record of the red bamboo building, which was widely circulated for a time. In Equator in the Congo of Africa, the equator zone, the heat is stifling, and people are prone to dizziness. Fortunately, the area produces fragrant bamboo. The trunk and branches are cut and ground into powder. Smelling it, the aroma is strong, resembling eaglewood and sandalwood, and it is cool and refreshing, relieving dizziness. The residents often carry a pouch around their waist, which is always filled with fragrant bamboo powder. Heaven's creation of things adapts to local conditions. It is truly amazing.

The Witty Remarks at the Wang and Li Tangbing Banquet 114

— Wu Fei

Ms. Wang Xiaoying, the principal of Wuben Girls' Middle School, gave birth to a son last month. All of her colleagues at the school offered their congratulations. On the 15th of this month [March], Principal Wang and Mr. Li Dachao held a Tangbing banquet at Zhongshe. Near noon, dozens of male and female colleagues arrived one after another. The seats were arranged in a straight line, facing each other. The chairman was at both ends. After taking their seats, everyone toasted the hostess to express their congratulations. Then, Mr. Lu Xun'an was publicly elected to give a speech on behalf of everyone. He began by saying that the great virtue of heaven and earth is birth. Everything in the world is born of each other in order to survive in society. Therefore, human life is also divided into three major periods. The first period is the period of being born and being protected. The second period is the period of giving birth. The third period is the period of implementing protection, having fulfilled the responsibility of giving birth. Principal Wang has moved from the second period and is about to enter the third period. She has fulfilled her national duty for her family, for her country, and for society. This is the so-called implementation of nationalism. Moreover, our country's old customs often regard the ability to glorify ancestors and benefit future generations as the virtue of the family. Principal Wang celebrated her father's birthday a month ago, offering toasts and showing respect. She can be said to have glorified her ancestors. Now she has the joy of giving birth to a son, isn't this benefiting future generations? Moreover, Principal Wang's name is Xiaoying. Xia means to be filial to one's parents. Ying means to enjoy educating talents. Principal Wang is filial to her parents, so her name is truly in line with reality. She also enjoys educating talents while managing school affairs. Now she enjoys educating the talents of others, and soon she will enjoy educating the talents of her own child. In a few years, there will be another little talent in the kindergarten of Wuben School. This is another reason to congratulate Principal Wang. The local scenery combined formality and humor. The listeners all applauded, saying it was a witty remark. Mr. Lu has a great eloquence and is also a heavy drinker. The only one who can match him is Mr. Wu Jingzhi. They were drinking face to face when the host, Mr. Dachao, arrived. Mr. Li is handsome and wears a Western suit. He is like Xu Gong from the northern part of the city. Mr. Lu got up to offer a toast. Mr. Li declined, saying he was not a good drinker. He was forced to drink again. He finally drank a cup, and his cheeks were already slightly flushed. Principal Wang said, "I knew he couldn't drink." It was already past three o'clock, and the banquet was coming to an end. Only someone had to leave early due to other matters. I believe the host and guests enjoyed themselves and were extremely happy.

A Short Account of the Jinde Amusement Fair 115

— Huo Gong

The Jinde Savings Society was initiated by gentlemen in Shanghai's gentry and business circles who advocated thrift and virtue. Initially, they rented a few simple houses to establish the society. The members were as few as morning stars. Before long, the society gradually developed, and the number of members increased daily. The original address was insufficient, so they relocated to larger houses several times. The public held an optimistic view of the society. After Mr. Chen Fukang was elected as the chief director, he devoted himself diligently to the management. With the support of his younger brother, Zenglin, and the old staff members, Li and Zheng, the society flourished even more. People from all walks of life joined like water flowing westward. As a result, they raised substantial funds to build their own premises on Laobaizi Road, Fusheng Road, occupying several acres of land with hundreds of rooms. Apart from allocating a portion for the Baixing Theater and Baixing Restaurant, there were many remaining rooms, divided into departments with orderly operations. In Shanghai, a city known for its extravagance, the society stood out for advocating thrift and virtue. Those with shallow views could not help but criticize it inwardly. The reason for its success was that it stood clean among the muddy, and things would inevitably revert to their opposite when they reached an extreme. Just like those who ate delicacies and fresh, fatty foods every day, they would inevitably find the taste of plain vegetables delightful when they occasionally had them. Yesterday, the society held a grand amusement fair specifically for expanding the physical education department. Hundreds of guests gathered together. The amusement program included the clear voices of Mr. Cai Defen, Mr. Tang Bolin, and Mr. Chen Fuli (Yang Cuixi), and the Jinde Orchestra's performance of Chinese music (General's Command, Farewell My Concubine). The zithers, pipa, and other musical instruments used were antique, elegant, and pleasing. Their cold sound was especially full of charm. Mr. Chen Taixun's Cantonese opera (Green Banana) had an excellent title, but I didn't understand the singing. As a native of Anhui, although I had worked with Cantonese people and my deceased wife, Ji Lanjiu, was from Guangdong, I only knew a little about ordinary Cantonese. However, I didn't understand Cantonese opera. The music used was also good, but I was outside the gate and couldn't name it. Ms. Xue Qian's Chinese martial arts were as swift as a rabbit and as agile as a soaring dragon. I, Dong Mei, am ashamed to face this female warrior. Mr. Zheng Laosheng and Mr. Wu Guanhua's Cantonese music dance was lively, humorous, and funny. I repeatedly burst into laughter. The Rose Society's magic show was incredibly clever with the ability to transform things on the spot. The act of sawing a living person in half was particularly astonishing. The fashion show featuring female stars Bai Meifang, Wang Meimei, Huang Lilin, Zhao Suqin, and Chen Ailun, with their fair skin, black eyebrows, and green makeup, arranged in groups of three or five, moving with light steps and swaying slender waists, was truly enviable. The harmonica performance by the Chinese Harmonica Society was able to create new sounds with children's toys, which was quite unexpected. Their march, with such small objects, simulated the galloping of thousands of troops, sometimes far and sometimes near, with clear distinctions in pitch, which could not be described as anything but a unique skill. Mr. Zhu Shiliang, Yang Nanying, Cao Zhenkang, Zhang Shiyang, Fang Yulin, Sun Junqing, Xia Pinpu, Wang Yiqing, Jin Runchu, Dai Baocheng, Lu Shaoan, and Tang Yunqing's Peking Opera performances, with their singing, acting, fighting, and martial arts, each excelled in their respective areas, which was not easy to come by from amateur performers. Yang Nanying's "Cosmic Front" was particularly commendable because a Fujianese singing Peking Opera, with his pronunciation and tone delivery, was surprisingly accurate and full of flavor, beyond my expectations. Moreover, he was an amputee (he was born without a right arm, and the one he supported in his sleeve was a prosthetic arm), so his performance should not have been worth watching. Unexpectedly, he drove the prosthetic arm as if it were a real hand, performing body movements such as wanting to ascend to the sky and enter the earth, which felt lively and natural, without any artificial traces. The most amazing thing was that the famous actor Yang Baosen did not appear on stage himself but played the qin for Nanying, without a single flaw from beginning to end, and followed the tune with perfect precision. Even an experienced qin player could not have surpassed him. This, along with Nanying's one-armed performance, could be called two great feats. The Ping Opera critic Zheng Guoyi followed Baosen closely, never leaving his side, which was what was called a special follower. Haha.

▲ Brief News: Cantonese singing and dancing star Violet recently arrived in Yindu (phonetic transliteration). The welcoming crowd was so enthusiastic that the entire city seemed to be in a frenzy. Violet, accompanied by her mother, Ms. Ma, visited her old comrades from the Tongmenghui and important figures of the National Government. She was so busy with social engagements that she had hardly any free evenings. When Mr. Tang, the manager of the National Grand Theater, heard about this, he invited her to perform on stage to entertain the people of the capital. Violet's trip to the capital was solely for sightseeing, and all her costumes and props were left in Shanghai. Therefore, she specially sent someone to Shanghai to take care of them. She will begin performing for three days starting on the 14th, featuring Cantonese operas such as "Mei Fei's Burial of Flowers" and "Chen Miaochang," as well as various dances. (Ru Jia)

Warmth in the Heart (383) 116

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Seventeen: Preserving Youth with Secret Arts, Blurring Eyebrows with Dark Colors; Seeking Destiny without Method, Buying Swift Horses in the Golden Market

It turned out that Hua Yuanchun was a familiar figure in Jiangnan, and this Grandma Pan was also from Changshu. They were fellow villagers. Grandma Pan's husband was a famous actor in Shanghai named Pan Xiaoqiao. After Grandma Pan received the telegram, she had no choice. The person was already dead, and it was a long way from Shanghai to Beijing. The travel expenses alone would cost one or two hundred yuan. Even if she went, she would only see a coffin. So she wrote a quick letter, naturally thanking Third Young Master Ye for taking care of the funeral arrangements. Old Sixth had a life of hardship, but in the end, she met Third Young Master Ye, which could be considered a bit of luck in her ill-fated life. However, her coffin was left alone in the north, which seemed too pitiful. It would be best to find a way to bring her back to Shanghai. Although Hua Lao Liu had a short and unfortunate life, she was still a person of her time. To abandon such a beautiful woman in the desolate northern suburbs seemed somewhat inappropriate. After Ye Tonghou received the letter, he said, "If you're going to help Buddha, you have to help him all the way to the West." He decided to transport her coffin to Shanghai. Once it was in Shanghai, he couldn't take care of it anymore. Fortunately, Hua Lao Liu had her lovers and close sisters in Shanghai, and they would naturally do their part. Ye Tonghou had extensive connections and knew many people. He entrusted a friend from a transportation company to transport Hua Yuanchun's coffin from the train to Tianjin and then from Tianjin to Shanghai on a China Merchants Bureau steamer. This matter spread throughout the alleys of Beijing. Third Young Master Ye earned a reputation for chivalry, especially among the girls in the south and north, who all said that Third Young Master Ye had a good heart. Many guests who had been friends in the past later became strangers, abandoning her like discarded items. Moreover, everyone knew that Third Young Master Ye and Hua Lao Liu did not have any physical relationship, so this was indeed not easy. Readers should know that Ye Tonghou also died in Beijing later on. At that time, his situation was very difficult, and it was a sudden illness. It was just as he and Hua Lao Liu had said at the beginning, "I won't die in Beijing." At that time, the funeral arrangements were rushed, and several girls from the south who knew Ye San wanted to come forward to do the funeral arrangements for Ye Tonghou. Fortunately, Ye Tonghou had an uncle who was a government official in the Ministry of Education and said that it was not appropriate and declined everything. However, these girls still invited a high monk to chant scriptures for three days to help him ascend to heaven. Although it involved superstition, it showed their sincerity. Who said that people in the brothels are all unfeeling and disregard righteousness? The matter of Hua Yuanchun was finally concluded. However, there was still a small ripple. It turned out that when her coffin was transported to Shanghai, there was a small dispute because Grandma Pan and Hua Lao Liu were good sisters and knew that Hua Lao Liu had a pair of joyful enemies in Shanghai. They had to give them a message. So she reported to her two lovers as if sending out a funeral announcement.

Business News

Gold and Gold Prices Finally Rise 117

Increase of Sixteen Taels and Seven Mace

Still Strong Fluctuations: Yesterday, March 17th, the gold price fell and then rose again, with strong fluctuations and an extremely complex market situation. A sudden storm was unavoidable. Standard Flour Market Rebounds 127

Yesterday, after the opening of the Standard Flour market in the morning, the market showed weakness in all months. Although the quotations from foreign markets rebounded by one, two, or three jiao, the environment remained unfavorable, and the price of gold also reported a heavy fall. Therefore, most people's sentiment remained weak. The prices for March, April, and May were slightly lower than the previous day by 0.01 fen, while the prices for June, July, and August all reached the 2.1 liang level. July even reached 1.9975 liang, indicating the weakness of market sentiment. However, the market sentiment suddenly changed after the opening of the market in the afternoon. With the sharp fall and then sharp rise in gold prices, temporary short positions rushed to cover their positions. Therefore, both near and far term contracts rebounded, with prices increasing by one or two fen from the morning's lowest price. However, from the perspective of recent bearishness, this partial rebound is still difficult to sustain. As a result, the price for the current month increased by 0.05 fen compared to the previous day, the price for April and May increased by 0.01 fen, and the price for June increased by 0.025 fen. The prices for July and August both increased by 0.05 fen.

Lush Tea Continues to Sell Well at Luzhuang 130

Yesterday, the trading of lush Zhenmei green tea from Luzhuang continued to be brisk. Tongfu, Jinlong, Baochang, Fushi, and other firms all began to search for goods. The Russian Aid Society also slightly increased its interest. Total transactions in the city amounted to over 700 boxes. Zhenmei was sold at a top price of 68 liang, Gongzhu was sold at 30 liang, Mazhu was sold at 50 liang, and Xiumei was sold at 13 liang. The market prices were all unchanged compared to the previous day. However, with only over 10,000 boxes remaining in the market, the market has stabilized.

Piece Goods: Eastern Goods' Prices Plummet 131

The market for cotton cloth from this factory has been depressed for days. The sharp fall in cotton yarn prices has prompted selling, leading to a downward trend. Prices are extremely chaotic, with distinctions between new and old goods. Among them, heavy-weight coarse cloth is relatively firm, with little downward movement. 16-yard Five Yuan Bao coarse twill is also quite firm due to the scarcity of spot goods. The rest are all weakening. Fine twill has fallen by about 0.01 yuan compared to before. Although fine cloth merchants are still searching for goods, it is difficult to reverse the trend. Caiqiu, Laba, Tongyanghe have all fallen to around 7.2 liang. 11-pound coarse cloth from Ewo is sold at 5.4 liang. 13-pound One Bullhead is the cheapest, sold at 5.9 liang. Ewo's blue striped bleached cloth and Gold Pagoda bleached cloth have all fallen.

Since the fall in the gold market, the price drop of Eastern and Western piece goods has been unprecedented. Western goods can still be maintained, while Eastern goods have plummeted. Straight Tribute Serge, Fine Drill, Zhongshan Serge, etc., have fallen by 0.025 to 0.05 yuan per day. The reason is that the sharp fall in the Eastern exchange rate has made Osaka's prices lower than Shanghai's. Merchants from Tianjin, Shantou, and Yunnan are no longer purchasing in Shanghai. Merchants from Sichuan and Hankou are unanimously watching, while only merchants from Changsha and Jiangxi are slightly replenishing their stocks. The price of Lake Heart Pavilion Drill has fallen by 0.32 yuan. Old Pattern Straight Tribute Serge 0.365 yuan. Half Moon Goose fine cloth has fallen by one liang compared to the beginning of the month, sold at 9.25 liang yesterday. Bleached cloth has also fallen.

Today's March 18th Commemoration 134

The Municipal Executive Committee will today (the 18th) commemorate the massacre of revolutionary citizens of Beiping by the Beiyang warlords under Duan Qirui's government five years ago in resistance to imperialism. The Shanghai Special Municipality Executive Committee has issued a public notice to raise awareness among all sectors.

County Reorganization Committee: The Shanghai County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee will hold a memorial ceremony in the auditorium of the committee at 10:00 a.m. today (the 18th) to commemorate the Beiping citizens' revolution. Notices have been sent to all agencies requesting their timely attendance.

Zhang Weicheng Discusses China-Korea Trade 135

Urgent Need to Promote Huachou and Xiabu: Zhang Weicheng, the Consul-General stationed in Korea, who has reported on the handling of negotiations over the past year, stayed at the Ongzhou Hotel on Lafayette Road while passing through Shanghai on his way to Beijing. Yesterday, he spoke to a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency about the commercial situation between China and Korea, as well as the situation of overseas Chinese. The annual trade volume between China and Korea is about 155 million yuan, with products from the three northeastern provinces accounting for the majority, accounting for eight-tenths of the total. In the past, silk was an important export item, but it has almost disappeared in the last two or three years because the Japanese government stipulated that the tax rate for Japanese silk transported to Korea was only 8%, while the tax rate for Chinese silk transported to Korea was as high as 100%. Although the new tariff agreement has reduced the tax to 70%, the difference is still large. However, Koreans are well aware that Chinese silk is durable. No matter how Japanese silk imitates Chinese silk patterns, Koreans' trust in Japanese silk is still not as good as their trust in Chinese silk. Therefore, Chinese silk merchants should seize the opportunity of this tariff reduction to quickly catch up and try to transport and sell silk to continue the previous status of Chinese silk in Korea. Otherwise, in another three or four years, Koreans will not know that there is Chinese silk, and the sales of Chinese silk in Korea will be permanently cut off. In addition, summer cloth is a common item for Koreans to wear, and China can also try to promote it. Currently, there are self-operated shipping lines from Yantai to Korea, and transportation is also more convenient. I have advised the shipping company to further expand to help Chinese and Korean businesses achieve mutual assistance and development. There are a large number of overseas Chinese in Korea. Since the ban on farmers and workers from Japan going to Korea was lifted after negotiations, more people have been going from the three northeastern provinces and Shandong. Koreans have a very good feeling towards China. Koreans feel that the cost of living in Korea is high, and the number of people moving to China in recent years is also very considerable. It is said that Mr. Zhang will go to Beijing tonight and stay in Beijing for about four or five days. He must return to Shanghai for a trip. His reception hours are from 9:00 a.m. to 10:00 a.m. and from 5:00 p.m. to 6:00 p.m.

Shanghai County Relocation Design Conference 136

Compensation of 90 yuan per mu for requisitioned land: The Shanghai County Relocation Design Committee held its fourth meeting at the County Government Auditorium at 10:00 a.m. yesterday. The meeting was attended by committee members Wu Wenhua, Director of the Construction Bureau; Wang Li, Director of the Finance Bureau (represented by Lu Dingxin); Shi She, Director of the Education Bureau; Ye Dezhen, Secretary of the County (represented by Yu Lingfen); Shen Zhou, Deputy Director of the Property Management Office; Lu Zhe, Committee Member of the County Reorganization Committee; Peng Zhaotang, District Chief of the Second District; Yang Fulin, District Chief of the Third District; Ge Xiusheng, District Chief of the Fifth District; and local gentry Peng Lirendeng. After Chairman Wu Wenhua conducted the ceremony, he first reported that an opinion letter on the location of the county government had been submitted to the county government for review by experts. Now, according to instructions, it has been decided that the location of the county government will be northwest of Humin Road and north of Hui Road. Second, the preliminary schedule for the relocation of the county has been drafted by the Construction Bureau and submitted to the 57th County Government Meeting for amendment and approval, and the county government has ordered compliance. The following resolutions were made: 1. The location of the county government has been determined, and a resolution was made on how to prepare for the survey of the county government area. The resolution was that the county government should be requested to order the Construction Bureau to complete the survey by the end of March. 2. A resolution was made on the standard price per mu for requisitioned land should be determined in advance. The resolution was that when land within the designated area is requisitioned, the compensation will be 90 yuan per mu. 3. The relocation funds are urgently needed. The old county government base and houses have been purchased by the Shanghai Municipal Government, and it is proposed to request the county government to ask for prompt allocation of funds to facilitate progress. The resolution was approved. 4. A resolution was made on how to prepare for the design of the new county government pattern. The resolution was to request the county government to order the Construction Bureau to handle it as soon as possible. 5. A resolution was made on whether to appoint a committee to be responsible for the requisition of land. The resolution was to appoint Wang Li, Wu Wenhua, and Yang Fulin to be responsible for handling the matter. 6. A resolution was made on the budget for the new county government. The resolution was to appoint Wu Wenhua to prepare a draft budget for discussion at the next meeting. 7. A resolution was made on whether to announce the land requisition map in advance. The resolution was to determine the announcement before April 10.

Results of Public Concession's Foreign Board Election 137

Old Directors Re-Elected: The election of the nine foreign directors of the Public Concession Bureau of Works concluded yesterday with the following results: Fukushima (Japan, 1086 votes), Okamoto (Japan, 1086 votes), Macnaghten (UK, 965 votes), Shepherd (UK, 904 votes), Carney (US, 884 votes), Hsu Shih (UK, 872 votes), Bland (UK, 860 votes), Peill (UK, 855 votes), and Raven (US, 795 votes). A total of 1247 votes were cast, with 18 invalid ballots. Japanese voters were the most enthusiastic. There were ten candidates for the board, and the nine elected were all old directors. Arnold was the only incumbent director who was not re-elected. As for the five Chinese directors, they will be re-elected by the Chinese Taxpayers Association and are expected to be re-elected as a whole.

French Aviators Still Did Not Arrive Yesterday 138

Landed in Shantou En Route: The two French aviators, Bairdan and Manez, who are flying a Farman monoplane on a long-distance flight from Paris to Tokyo, were stranded in Hong Kong for two days due to heavy fog. Yesterday morning, the weather in Hong Kong had still not improved, but the French aviators decided not to delay any longer and took off from Hong Kong at 9:40 a.m. yesterday, risking their flight to Shanghai. Upon hearing the news, the French Consulate General and Chinese and foreign journalists in the city went to Hongqiao Airport to welcome them. Responsible personnel from the Aviation Administration and the Municipal Public Security Bureau also arrived at the airport to take care of the situation. French Consul General Coglin, Chief of the Political Department of the French Police Station Shao Chengziqing, and several French priests were all at Hongqiao Airport to welcome them. According to news from the French Consulate General, the French aviators were expected to arrive around 6:30 p.m. However, at that time, the northeast wind was very strong and the sky was overcast. Although the welcoming people knew that the French aviators had departed from Hong Kong, they were doubtful whether they could fly to Shanghai in such bad weather. After waiting for a long time until late in the evening at 6:00 p.m., the French Consulate General received a telegram from Shantou that the French aviators had finally been forced to land in Shantou due to weather conditions. The welcomers at Hongqiao Airport received a telephone notification from the French Consulate General and returned disappointed. If the weather improves today, the French aviators can fly to Shanghai from Shantou this afternoon. It is also heard that whether the French aviators will fly to Nanjing or Beiping after arriving in Shanghai is still under negotiation, otherwise, they may go to Tokyo via Shenyang or Korea.

China National Aviation Corporation's Beijing-Ping Aviation Line Scheduled 139

Implemented on April 1st

Wireless Telegraph to be Installed

Timetable and Fares Determined

The five stations along the Beijing-Ping route of the China National Aviation Corporation have been prepared. The test flights have been successful, and both Chinese and foreign pilots are competent. The official opening date has been set for April 1st, with two-way flights once a day after 8:00 a.m. The aircraft is a Stinson model. The information obtained from yesterday's investigation is recorded as follows:

Installation of Wireless Telegraph: The wireless telegraphs required for each station along the route have been ordered from Shanghai by the company. The Beijing telegraph, with a capacity of 1,000 watts, has been transported and installed. The Xuzhou and Tianjin telegraphs, with a capacity of 200 watts, have also been transported and are being installed. The Jinan telegraph, with a capacity of 500 watts, is currently in Shanghai and will be shipped soon. The capital has the original telegraph of the Aviation Administration, with the same wattage as Beijing. The stations are all installed by our country's engineers.

Timetable for Each Station: The company has set the official opening date very close. General Manager He Jiwu ordered the business group to formulate the Beijing-Ping northbound and southbound flight timetables, which were drafted yesterday and will be submitted to the aviation group for implementation. Northbound flights depart from Nanjing at 8:30 a.m., arrive in Xuzhou at 10:30 a.m., depart from Xuzhou at 10:40 a.m., arrive in Jinan at 12:30 p.m., depart from Jinan at 12:40 p.m., arrive in Tianjin at 2:35 p.m., depart from Tianjin at 2:45 p.m., and arrive in Beijing at 3:30 p.m. Southbound flights depart from Beijing at 8:00 a.m., arrive in Tianjin at 8:45 a.m., depart from Tianjin at 8:55 a.m., arrive in Jinan at 10:50 a.m., depart from Jinan at 11:00 a.m., arrive in Xuzhou at 12:50 p.m., depart from Xuzhou at 1:00 p.m., and arrive in Beijing at 3:10 p.m.

One-Way and Round-Trip Fares: The company has set the one-way and round-trip fares for the Beijing-Ping route. The one-way fare from Beijing to Beijing is 150 yuan, and the round-trip fare is 225 yuan. The one-way fare from Beijing to Xuzhou, Jinan, or Tianjin is 44 yuan per station, and the round-trip fare is 60 yuan. The one-way fare from Tianjin to Beijing is 18 yuan, and the round-trip fare is 27 yuan. The prices are subject to approval by the board of directors.

He Jiwu's Talk: A reporter from Guowen News Agency interviewed Mr. He Jiwu, the general manager of the company, yesterday to inquire about his views on the aviation plan. Mr. He replied that people who have not traveled by plane consider air travel to be dangerous. Once they have traveled by plane, they find it unremarkable, and the time savings for passengers are considerable. At first glance, the fare seems higher than traveling by train, but it should be understood that time is money. The company is very strict in reviewing drivers and personnel. All Chinese and foreign technicians hired for each aircraft must be reviewed by the aviation group director Smith to ensure that they have considerable driving experience before they can be employed. The official Beijing-Ping aviation service will be implemented on April 1st. The company plans to expand its routes to develop its business. After the Beijing-Ping route is opened, it will prepare the Shanghai-Guangdong route. After that, it will gradually extend to the South Pacific Islands. In January, it will actively train Chinese aviation technicians and those interested in practicing aviation technology in preparation for future needs and for the provision of subsidies. The training director will be Smith.

Price Increase for Yangtze River Steamer Alliance 144

Hankou Merchants' Opposition: A Statement to Shanghai Shipping Merchants Regarding the Yangtze River Six Companies' Business Alliance and Fare Increase, which has aroused universal opposition from the Hankou Customs Brokers, who denounce it as humiliating the nation and forfeiting its rights. Shanghai's Chinese merchant ships view business cooperation and the recovery of navigation rights as two separate matters, with the latter being more eagerly anticipated by the Chinese shipping community. It is unrealistic to expect two or three Chinese ships to shoulder this heavy responsibility. Therefore, yesterday, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, San Peh Steam Navigation Company, Ning Shao Steam Navigation Company, and other companies jointly decided to send a reply telegram to the Hankou Customs Brokers Association, detailing the discussion on the recovery of navigation rights and business cooperation. This matter is of great importance and is recorded in detail as follows:

Freight Rates Increased: Since the proposal for business cooperation among the Yangtze River Six Companies, the specific method of profit sharing has not yet been determined, so it is still under negotiation. However, implementation is inevitable, merely a matter of time. Regarding fare increases, a preliminary agreement has been reached, and starting yesterday, all six companies have uniformly increased rates. In addition to abolishing shallow water fees, all cargo rates have been increased by about 30%. Freight rates for both upstream and downstream cargo will be charged at the new prices. The reason for the increase is not due to cooperation, but rather the substantial increase in expenses due to gold price increases, making it a necessity given the circumstances. Merchants in Shanghai have already been paying the new rates.

Hankou Merchants Oppose: Upon hearing about the cooperation and fare increase by the Six Companies, the Hankou Customs Brokers Association held a special meeting to oppose it. The Yangtze River Six Steamship Companies were considered by China, England, and Japan to be a move by Chinese shipping merchants to accommodate foreigners. Therefore, a telegram was sent to the central government requesting a ban, and another telegram was sent to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, San Peh Steam Navigation Company, and Ning Shao Steam Navigation Company, stating that the Six Companies' business alliance was humiliating the nation and forfeiting its rights, harming both merchants and civilians. Details have been submitted to the central government for review, requesting a halt to its progress. Sincerely, Hankou Customs Brokers Association.

The Three Companies' Reply: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Ning Shao Steam Navigation Company, and San Peh Steam Navigation Company have consulted multiple times on this matter and drafted a reply telegram, which was sent out yesterday. It roughly stated: "Your telegram has been received. We have investigated that the Six Companies' agreement on fare prices is an old practice from the past, the main purpose of which is to avoid competition among peers and follow market customs, just as your association regards the registration of foreign ships as a common practice. There is no evil intent to harm Chinese merchants or forfeit national rights. If your association truly believes that the joint pricing of Chinese and foreign shipping merchants is inappropriate, then you should guarantee that all Chinese merchants unite and completely refuse to load foreign ships, which would be the right approach. However, now that foreign ships operating within the country have become dominant, their capital is abundant, and they can compete fiercely, which cannot be matched by two or three Chinese shipping companies. Therefore, to address the root of the problem, it is necessary to recover navigation rights and support the domestic shipping industry. While support still largely depends on the government's efforts, it also relies on the collective efforts of various merchant groups to provide mutual assistance and safeguard the industry. This time, Chinese and foreign shipping merchants are combining due to circumstances. If our patriotic merchants can unite firmly and happily choose Chinese shipping, refusing to load foreign ships, then those foreign ships with abundant capital and strength will also be helpless and unable to exert their skills. Otherwise, temporary competition and sacrifices will only lead to the destruction of domestic shipping and the profiteering of unscrupulous merchants, which will not contribute to national sovereignty or the interests of the people. Moreover, at a time when gold prices are soaring and expenses are increasing sharply, if foreign ships are not constrained by Chinese ships, their fare increases will not stop at these levels. Therefore, looking to the future, if there are no two or three Chinese shipping companies mediating, foreign ships in China will become more rampant in their monopolistic control. The harm to our Chinese merchants and the humiliation of our national rights will be unimaginable. If your association has sound and concrete plans for maintaining Chinese shipping and safeguarding national rights, our company is willing to be instructed. We do not know how your association will guide us."

Special Shipping News 145

French Ship Aground: According to news from the French Consulate in Shanghai, the French postal ship "Yangtze" was sailing between Vietnam and Shanghai. Yesterday, while passing through the waters off Zhejiang Province, the ship ran aground on a reef at Bei Yu Shan (transliteration). It is reported that all cargo is safe. Upon learning of this, the French Consulate immediately ordered a French warship to communicate with the stranded postal ship via radio and arrange for rescue.

Japanese Ship Accident: The Sixth Shen Sheng Maru of the Japanese Dalian Shen Sheng Steamship Company, which was transporting coal from Hongji to Shanghai, encountered fog on the morning of the 14th in the South Sea Strait and ran aground on a reef. The bottom of the ship was breached, and seawater has flooded the deck. The crew and sailors are still missing. A Japanese fishing boat is on site to provide rescue. It was reported yesterday that many items on board have been looted by pirates. The Japanese warship "Uji," which was in Guangdong, has sailed to the area to rescue and search for the crew.

Chang Xing Damaged: The San Peh Company's Chang Xing ship was loading cargo at the company's wharf in the southern city yesterday when the Ning Shao ship returned to Shanghai from the Yangtze River and docked at the wharf. Due to strong winds and waves, the ship was impacted by the waves and collided with the Chang Xing ship. The outer hull of the Chang Xing's front cabin was damaged, and the iron plates were destroyed. Fortunately, it was above the waterline. The company was immediately notified to send personnel to inspect and repair it. The ship sailed to Hankou as usual this morning.

World Ship Arrives: The German Hamburg Company sends a world cruise ship to China every year. This year, the 20,000-ton giant ship "Lissaro" has been assigned, carrying a world travel group of over 300 people. It is coming from New York via Europe to Shanghai. Yesterday, a telegram was received stating that the ship has arrived in Hong Kong and is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 27th of this month. After staying in Shanghai for one day, it will sail to Japan, cross the Pacific Ocean, and return to the United States.

Zheng Zhensheng Dies in Western Prison After the May 30th Massacre 146

Plaintiff's Attempt at Reconciliation Fails: The Deceased's Wife Reports to the Seamen's Union. The Daily News reports: After the May 30th Massacre in the fourteenth year [of the Republic of China, i.e., 1925], all sectors of society responded with fervor. The Shanghai seamen planned a strike to provide assistance, but it was obstructed by Wang Zhongqing, the head of the "living fire" contractor. The strike committee, on the afternoon of June 6th at 1:00 PM, ordered seaman Zheng Zhensheng to assassinate Wang Zhongqing at No. 2009 Xinji Bang Road to ensure the strike would be successful. The assassination failed, and Zheng was arrested and sent to the joint court for trial. He was sentenced to five years and sent to the Western Prison. Zheng's wife, Mrs. Chai, petitioned for probation and filed appeals, but to no avail. When the National Revolutionary Army won the Northern Expedition and established its capital in Nanjing, Zheng Zhensheng managed to send a letter from prison and dispatched someone to see Shao Lizi and Ye Chucang, requesting their assistance. The Seamen's Union also petitioned the central government to redress the injustice. The official documents that went back and forth were numerous, but the release was delayed. Last autumn, the five-year term expired, but Zheng remained imprisoned. The Seamen's Union again petitioned the central government to demand his release, but it was not carried out. On the 3rd of this month, Zheng's family suddenly received a notice from the Western Prison stating that Zheng Zhensheng had died on the 25th of last month. The coffin containing the body has been placed in the Ningbo Guild Hall at the North Station. Soon after, Wang Zhongqing, the plaintiff, sent someone to negotiate with Zheng's wife, Mrs. Chai, offering to pay her 40 yuan per month as a form of reconciliation until Zheng's son reached the age of sixteen, at which point the payments would cease. Mrs. Zheng refused and reported to the Seamen's Union, requesting redress. The Seamen's Union held a meeting the day before yesterday and decided to again petition the central government to open Zheng Zhensheng's coffin for examination to verify the circumstances.

Case of a Worker Injured by White Russian at Aid Organization 147

Declaration from the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association of Workers at the French Water and Electricity Company

The Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association of Workers at the French Water and Electricity Company issues a public announcement to all sectors of society regarding the tragic case of Liu Jinshan, a worker at the Lomeck Sugar Factory: Beloved workers, respected members of all sectors of society, a shocking and outrageous tragedy occurred at 8:30 AM on the 11th of this month at the Lomeck Sugar Factory, which is owned by White Russian capitalists on Da Xi Road. The incident was caused when a White Russian named Miliuosike, who was employed by the factory, took a wiping cloth that worker Liu Jinshan had washed. When worker Liu asked to see it, this White Russian, who was usually directed and favored by the factory owner, had been oppressing and bullying workers for more than a day. At this time, he punched worker Liu violently in the ear several times. Worker Liu was seriously injured and fell to the ground, bleeding profusely and losing consciousness. He was sent to the Red Cross Hospital for examination. According to the hospital report, his eardrum was ruptured, his auditory nerve was severed, and his brain was injured, endangering his life. If worker Liu dies, he leaves behind an elderly mother in her sixties with white hair and a young wife with two children under the age of five, all of whom depend on worker Liu to provide for them with the money he earns from his blood and sweat. The assailant has directly injured worker Liu personally and indirectly harmed his entire family. The cries of the elderly mother for her son, the young wife for her husband, and the two children for their father are unbearable to hear. This situation is intolerable! The White Russian has been arrested by the police, and the court has scheduled a hearing for the 20th of this month. The factory workers are unanimously indignant. Worker Liu is a fellow-provincial from Hubei, and the workers from the same province at the sugar factory and his family came to our association to explain the circumstances. Upon hearing this, the workers at our association were extremely saddened and angered. The White Russian capitalists used cruel means to violently assault our worker. Alas, our worker was killed without reason at the factory. Since this dark and tragic incident has occurred, all our beloved workers and members of all sectors of society are heartbroken. This is not only a matter for our fellow-provincial worker from Hubei, but it is a personal tragedy for all workers in Shanghai. Our association solemnly declares to all labor unions, workers, and members of all sectors of society, demanding that we unite and strive to uphold human rights, expel the White Russians, and protect the safety of all workers in Shanghai. Our association proposes: (1) The factory owner must immediately compensate worker Liu for all losses. If there are any accidents, the capitalist should provide compensation and wait for further discussion on the arrangements. (2) We demand a guarantee of safety in the future to prevent similar incidents from occurring. (3) The assailant and the Lomeck factory owner who condoned the violence must be immediately punished. (4) We will initiate the organization of a support association for the Liu case. (5) The White Russians must be expelled from the factory. The above are the minimum measures, and we must unite and strive to the end. This is our announcement.

Second Day of the National Cotton Production Conference 149

The National Cotton Production Improvement and Statistics Conference continued its second general meeting at 8:00 AM yesterday, with over 50 representatives attending. Yang Xiandong chaired the meeting, and Ji Zifeng served as the recorder. The afternoon session began at 1:30 PM, chaired by Lu Feishu, with Chu Xiusheng and Zheng Huainian serving as recorders. The proceedings of the meeting are recorded as follows:

Reports: In the morning, representatives from Xidu Huan Tang, Jiangxi Zhang Yinqing, and Anhui Wang Jiqu, and in the afternoon, representatives from Jiangsu Hu Jingliang and Zhejiang Wu Weijing, reported on the cotton production, yield, quality, and other conditions of cotton farming in their respective provinces, as well as plans for improvement.

Speeches: In the morning, Mr. Sun Yushu spoke on the topic of "The Preservation of Purebred Varieties in the Promotion of Cotton Seeds." He emphasized three points for maintaining the purity of seeds: (1) using administrative methods for agricultural promotion; (2) using educational methods; and (3) hoping for public assistance in development. Regarding the promotion aspect, he suggested paying attention to: (1) demonstration cotton fields; (2) seeking guidance from agricultural households for teaching; and (3) increasing interest in seed selection to encourage it. In the afternoon, speakers included: (A) Mr. Feng Zhaochuan, who spoke on "Several Important Issues in Cotton Seed Improvement," with four main points: (1) studying the heredity of cotton crops; (2) the problem of natural cross-pollination in cotton crops; (3) breeding methods; and (4) fertilization management methods for cotton crops. (B) Mr. Chen Yanshan spoke on "The Origin, Process, and Hope for the 'Million' Variety of Cotton Developed by Jin Da": (1) It originated in the seventh year of the Republic [of China, i.e., 1918] when an American plant physiologist came to China to investigate and promote it, with the support of the Chinese Cotton Mill Owners Association. (2) The seeds of the "Million" cotton variety were brought to Wusong by Guo Renfeng in the eighth year of the Republic [of China, i.e., 1919]. The results were long fibers, strong luster, few impurities, and the ability to spin up to 42-count yarn. (3) He hoped that everyone could find even better seeds.

Two Review Committees: A total of 76 proposals were received for this conference by the 16th. The preliminary meeting decided to divide them into improvement and statistics groups. The improvement group elected Sun Yushu, Chen Yanshan, Li Lubin, Fang Junqiang, Zhang Zemin, Yuan Zhongyuan, Hu Pingchu, Zhao Lianfang (who resigned and was replaced by Feng Zhaochuan), and Ye Yuanding as the nine members of the proposal review committee for the improvement group. Sun Yushu convened the committee. The statistics group elected Jiang Dixian, Du Huan Tang, Liu Shushu, Wu Weijing, Chen Bingquan, Wang Jinwu, and Jiang Han Luo as the members of the compilation and review committee. Wang Jinwu convened the committee. The improvement group began reviewing the proposals the night before, merging 14 cases into four. The review of each case continued last night. The statistics group began reviewing last night.

Today's Agenda: The meeting will open at 9:00 AM today. Fang Junqiang will speak on "Rational Promotion." After the speech, the discussion on proposals (improvement group) will begin. In the afternoon at 1:30 PM, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry will host refreshments and a tour, and Mr. Ye Yuanding, director of the cotton yarn inspection department of the bureau, will speak on "Reforms in Chinese Cotton Inspection and the Improvement of the Cotton Industry."

Meeting of the Silk Factory Industry Relief Committee 150

Methods of Distributing Debt

The Special Committee for the Relief of the Silk Factory Industry in the Three Regions of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai held a plenary committee meeting yesterday (the 17th) at 3:00 PM at the Shanghai Silk Factory Industry Association. Those present included Shen Yichen, Wang Xiaolai, Chu Xuanzeng, Zhu Mouxian, Huang Jinfan, and ten others. Shen Yichen was elected as chairman. After formal greetings, the chairman announced the purpose of the meeting, and then the representatives who went to Beijing to petition for the second time reported on the petition process in Beijing. Chu Xuanzeng then spoke, saying that the matter of issuing silk public bonds was entrusted to him and Wang Xiaolai to petition in Beijing. He went to Beijing twice. For the second time, because Representative Wang was ill, Shen Yichen was appointed as the representative. He first visited the Ministers of Industry and Finance, and then hosted banquets for the members of the Executive and Legislative Yuan, as well as the Ministers of Finance and Industry, and other officials. He clearly stated the urgent situation of the silk factory industry, requesting that the original plan to issue 8 million yuan in bonds to provide relief be maintained. However, the plan has already been announced and implemented, making it difficult to change. The members and Minister Kong recognized that the European sales of the factories have weakened recently, and manufacturers are suffering heavy losses, which will lead to complete bankruptcy. The need for relief is urgent and cannot be delayed. Removing the expenses for improving mulberry trees and other things from the 6 million yuan in bond funds is not enough for distribution. They should show sympathy. As a result, they agreed to wait for our industry to submit a request to the Ministry of Finance and Industry, which will then be forwarded to the Executive and Legislative Yuan for review and approval to increase the bond amount. However, the procedure is very tight. Submitting requests through various channels takes time. The fastest would be three to four weeks before it can be announced and implemented. Next, the method of distributing the amount was discussed. Everyone agreed that the previously determined method of distributing according to the amount of silk in storage was no longer applicable due to time constraints. The best way would be to distribute according to the number of silk reeling machines, so that it would be fair and there would be no fraud. Regarding the organization of the public debt distribution committee, the court and ministry would send three people, the silk factory industry would send three people, and three people familiar with the silk industry would be hired, for a total of nine people to form the committee. It was decided to reserve this matter for discussion at the next committee meeting. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

The Shanghai Native Bank Association Notifies the National Industry 151

Please Unanimously Advocate for a Separate Native Bank Law

The Shanghai Native Bank Association, due to the difficulty of implementing the Banking Law, has already petitioned various agencies of the National Government to enact a separate Native Bank Law. Yesterday, it specially notified the industry across the country, stating: "We respectfully inform you that our Native Bank industry has a long history of circulating funds and supporting various industries, bearing a large task. This was true in the past, and it is even more so now. The reason why it has progressed repeatedly without failure is that it relies on an organization that is suitable for national conditions and the habit of strictly adhering to credit, which is known to the public. Now, we read in the newspaper that the Banking Law passed by the Legislative Yuan states in the final clause of the first article that 'those who operate one of the aforementioned businesses but do not call themselves banks are considered banks.' This means that our Native Bank industry is subordinate to banks. Furthermore, detailed translations of the various articles are not in accordance with the organization, customs, and business methods of our industry, or even contradict them greatly. If we do not comply, we will be suspected of violating the law. If we reluctantly comply, we will suffer hardship. Therefore, a meeting was held to resolve to petition the Central Political Council of the Chinese Kuomintang, the Chairman of the National Government, the Presidents of the Executive and Legislative Yuan, and the Ministers of Industry and Finance to carefully consider the situation and enact a separate Native Bank Law for compliance. However, this matter is of great importance, and our industry shares common interests. We should respond as quickly as possible. We have enclosed a draft for your review. We hope that you will use your insights to make requests in unison, so that the government will adopt them and establish a foundation for the Native Bank industry."

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Exemption from Increasing Third-Class Train Ticket Prices 152

Please Limit Price Increases to First and Second Class Tickets

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce wired the Ministry of Railways, stating: "Ministry of Railways, Nanjing. Recently, we heard that your ministry, in order to repay the principal and interest on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, as well as the increased costs of materials due to the value of gold, is considering increasing passenger ticket prices by 20% to compensate for the losses, and it is scheduled to be implemented on March 16th. We believe that clothing, food, housing, and transportation are the four essential elements of life. Recently, due to the value of gold, the costs of clothing, food, and housing, whether directly or indirectly from abroad, have been gradually increasing. As the newspapers have reported, it is difficult for ordinary people to find ways to make ends meet. The impact of the value of gold is a widespread phenomenon in society. The only difference is that public institutions can find other ways to supplement their funds, while ordinary people struggle to cope. Your ministry understands the hardship of the people. Once the affiliated associations make representations on their behalf, you should take it to heart. Moreover, the two railways are located in the center of industry and commerce. Due to the abnormal development of the city, many poor people from the interior flock to the city to make a living. The continuous flow of passengers has invisibly increased the benefits of the railway. There is no need to compensate by increasing prices. Even if public institutions suffer excessive losses and need to increase passenger ticket prices to make up for part of the losses, the situation of passengers traveling in third-class carriages is as described above. If transportation costs increase at the same time as the prices of clothing, food, and housing increase, the livelihoods of ordinary people will be more difficult, and society will become more chaotic. Therefore, the 35th Standing Committee Meeting of our association decided to request your ministry to increase the prices of first and second-class passenger tickets and to exempt third-class ticket prices to benefit the people. We respectfully present this case and request your consideration and approval for implementation."

As for domestic silkworm seeds, the season for silkworm rearing is approaching, and the silkworm seeds need to be distributed urgently. Japanese Fishing Vessels Using False Identification Numbers Seized 161

Iced Fish Has Become Rotten and Unfit for Consumption

Two Vessels Fined One Thousand Yuan, Two Vessels Confiscated

The Japanese fishing vessels No. 12 and No. 13, both named "Daiichi Daisei Maru," attempted to deceive authorities by using falsified identification numbers to enter and exit the Jianghai Customs area. Patrol officers (commonly known as "yellow boats") stationed at the Wusong Fort of the customs discovered the deception and seized both "Daiichi Daisei Maru" vessels. Subsequently, two more fishing vessels, "Ryobo Maru" and "Daihua Maru," arrived to collude and attempt an escape, but their scheme was uncovered, and they were also detained by the customs officers. Details were previously reported in this newspaper on August 2. It is now learned that the customs commissioner has approved the fine of one thousand yuan for "Daihua Maru" and "Ryobo Maru," and they have been released. Both "Daiichi Daisei Maru" vessels have been confiscated and will soon be put up for auction. However, the large quantity of iced fish stored in these two vessels has been delayed for so long that it has rotted in the holds and emitted an unbearable stench. Anyone passing near the vessels was nauseated for three days. Yesterday, the crew of the ships disposed of the stinking fish into the ocean to avoid affecting public health.

Numerous Disputes Regarding the Sichuan-Hankou Railway 166

Feng Lizhou and Zeng Xianzhi File Mutual Lawsuits

Although Zeng and Feng Have Sought Mediation

A Strategy for Fundamental Resolution Should Be Formulated

The dispute over shares in the Sichuan-Hankou Railway has repeatedly led to litigation. The railway company's former general manager, Zhang Taikai, was convicted by the Shanghai District Court for embezzling over three million yuan of public funds. Subsequently, a director of the company, Mr. Li, appointed Feng Lizhou as the resident manager in Hankou. However, Feng did not take office, and Ni Gongwei was appointed in his place. Recently, Feng suddenly filed a lawsuit with the Special District Court, accusing Zeng Xianzhi of harboring a fugitive. Zeng was arrested by the court police at a banquet in Xinghualou last week and was released on bail of one thousand yuan. As no one provided surety, Zeng was detained. The reason for the lawsuit against Zeng stems from an incident several years ago. Liu Yajue, also a director of the Sichuan Railway Company, was previously detained by the Beiping Prosecutor's Office after being sued by the shareholder maintenance association. Feng Lizhou bailed him out, but he subsequently fled without a trace. The Hebei High Court then confiscated the one thousand yuan bail paid by Feng and ordered the surrender of the bailed party. Now, Feng learned that Liu Yajue was being harbored by Zeng Xianzhi, so he filed a lawsuit against Zeng. Zeng, after being arrested, also filed a countersuit against Feng, stating that he and Liu Yajue were not on good terms, and Feng often met with Liu. Liu went to Chongqing and sent a letter to Feng to inform him. How could he, Zeng, have stopped Liu's actions? He was now being groundlessly accused by Feng, and he had not yet received the summons issued by the court, as Feng had colluded with others to forge his signature, causing the court to mistakenly believe that he had received the summons and intentionally failed to appear for the hearing, leading to the issuance of an arrest warrant. This conduct constitutes false accusation and defamation, and Feng should be punished. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Tingqi held a hearing on these mutual lawsuits. The lawyer for the plaintiff, Feng Lizhou, requested a postponement, stating that the case seemed amenable to mediation. The representative lawyer for the defendant, Zeng Xianzhi, replied that the Sichuan Railway litigation was extensive and complex, such as Ni Gongwei suing Feng Lizhou and the mutual lawsuit between Feng and Zeng. Since mediation was being considered, a strategy for fundamental resolution should be formulated to avoid tangential issues. However, Zeng Xianzhi has been unable to provide bail since his arrest and remains in custody. Now that mediation is underway, he requested that Zeng be allowed to post bail. Ni Gongwei was also in court and stood up to say that he was willing to provide bail for Zeng. Judge Wu then instructed Zeng Xianzhi to provide a surety who would appear whenever summoned. The guarantor must have a legitimate occupation. The case was adjourned for further hearing.

Hu Die's Reply Regarding Contract Termination Case 167

Sophistry Has No Value for Refutation

Only Awaiting Legal Judgment

Hu Die and Lin Xuehuai have been involved in litigation due to marital discord, which has recently turned into a war of words through mutual letters. Yesterday, lawyer Zhan Jifeng, representing Hu Die, replied to a letter from Lin Xuehuai's lawyers, Eson and Ni Jing'ao, stating that Miss Hu Die had seen in the newspapers that your client, Lin Xuehuai, had replied to Die's letter of the 14th of this month. Reading it, it is truly contemptible. Die's previous letter had already stated the facts and evidence, and sophistry is useless. Can deceit and trickery truly make people unable to distinguish right from wrong in this world? This kind of self-deceiving sophistry has no value for refutation. Now, a few points are selected to prove its fallacy: (1) Marriage between a man and woman is closely related to character and personality. For example, after a man and a woman are engaged, if it is discovered that the man is full of fraud and his behavior is despicable, the woman has a right to be cautious. How can marriage and character be considered separate matters? The letter refers to Die's reply as irrelevant and unresponsive, which shows a lack of common sense. (1) The accusation of emotional abandonment: it is clear that there have been two previous letters requesting the termination of the marriage contract. Now, the responsibility for unwarranted breach of contract is placed on Die, falsely accusing her of emotional abandonment. Is this what the letter calls justice? The claim that Die is surrounded by people is also noted. Die solemnly declares to the public that Die, being inexperienced in the world, was once deceived and surrounded. Now, she is trying to extricate herself from this situation to avoid future regrets. (1) The accusation that the evidence is fabricated: the matter that Die is pursuing is based entirely on evidence. Now that he knows he has no defense, he falsely accuses Die of fabricating the evidence. If this is true, why not file a criminal lawsuit? Is the crime of forging documents in Chapter 14 of the criminal law ineffective? In short, such false and deceptive words are too numerous to refute. Hereafter, we can only await legal judgment and have no time for further discussion. She entrusts this lawyer to reply and asks you to forward it. Sincerely, addressed to the two lawyers Eson and Ni Zheng'ao.

Establishment of the Siming Literature Solicitation Society 168

Office Located in the Ningbo Fellow Countrymen Association

Zhang Shenzhi, Li Jianhou, and other Ningbo fellow countrymen residing in Shanghai have established the Siming Literature Solicitation Society for the purpose of collecting Siming literature. A charter has been established for soliciting members. The office is temporarily located within the Ningbo Fellow Countrymen Association and is divided into six divisions: (1) Collection Division: Responsible for searching for lost and scattered literature. (2) Finance Division: Responsible for raising funds and promoting advance subscription tickets. (3) Review Division: Responsible for reviewing collected manuscripts. (4) Editing Division: Responsible for editing the books to be published. (5) Printing Division: Responsible for printing and proofreading matters. (6) Accounting Division: Responsible for revenue and expenditure. Three directors will be temporarily appointed, each concurrently serving as head of Collection & Finance, Review & Editing, and Printing & Accounting, respectively, to ensure accountability. The members of each division will be appointed by the society members. Meetings will be held once a month. It is reported that there are already twenty-eight members.

Fifteen Male and Female Bandits Committed One Kidnapping and Seven Robberies 170

The Robbery Cases Were Heard First Yesterday

Detectives Wang Runhe and Yang Zhaoqing, along with patrolman Zhang Faxiang, of the Hongkou Police Station, successively arrested fifteen bandits, including Shen A Si, Wu Shenxian, Ling Yongnian, Miao Caibao, Chen Azhang, Li Ruishan, Li Boying, Wang Songlin, Zhou Shisheng, Li A Ming, Cai Hongsheng (also known as Ma Pi Hongsheng), the woman Fei San Ai, Wu Shenshi, Ling Taoshi, Miao Wangshi, etc., and confiscated two handguns and fourteen bullets from the home of Ling Yongnian at 880 Shanhai Pass Road. They were sent to the Special District Court for questioning and investigation. It has now been determined that the defendants committed one kidnapping and seven robberies in the concession area, listed below: (1) On February 3 of this year, the home of Zhu Wenshan at 692 Tangjia Lane was robbed of property worth 2,299 yuan. (2) On February 27 of this year, the Gu Jinji store at 531 Qipu Road was robbed of 161 yuan. (3) On December 21 of last year, the home of Zhou Zhao Shi at 71 Xin Zha Road was robbed of 705 yuan. (4) On February 14 of this year, Zhang Li Shi at San Tai Road was robbed of 329 yuan. (5) On December 10 of last year, the home of Wang Cailin at Di Siwei Road was robbed of 436 yuan. (6) On September 22 of last year, the Yongchang Pawnshop on Avenue Road was robbed of 1,800 yuan. (7) On October 19 of last year, the home of Cai Guifu at Kangnaotuo Road was robbed of 1,300 yuan. (8) The defendants Shen A Si, Wu Shenxian, Wang Songlin, and Li A Ming kidnapped Chen Shifan, the owner of the Chen Lin Ji Construction Company, at 9 PM on December 19 of last year on Pingwang Street, Fuzhou Road, and hid him in newly built houses on the French Concession's La Du Road. The defendants received a ransom of 4,000 yuan for his release. Patrolman Zhang Yi of the Old Gate Police Station also apprehended another kidnapper, Lu A Gen, in room 301 of the Huizhong Inn on Hankou Road, who was found to be involved in the kidnapping of Chen Shifan. Yesterday afternoon, the police station, along with the victims, escorted the defendants to the Fifth Criminal Court of the Special District Court. The police lawyer presented the case, stating that Chen Shifan, the kidnapped victim, had not arrived, so the robbery cases should be heard first. The Chinese and Western detectives then explained the investigation process, followed by the victims testifying in turn, demonstrating the state of the robberies. Judge Feng Shide reviewed the confessions and ordered the defendants to be returned to custody separately, pending a rescheduled hearing.
