Water Patrol Team Discovers Kidnapping Bandits While Patrolling the River 172

Cai Huiqing, a villager from Nanjiazi Township in Yancheng, Jiangbei, had some farmland and savings, attracting the attention of bandits. In December of last year, Cai was delighted by the birth of his son and threw a grand banquet, attracting numerous guests. This attracted the attention of thieves. On the evening of December 22, Cai suddenly heard a series of loud cracking sounds outside the door. Immediately after, the wooden door was broken open by eight or nine violent thugs, who rushed in. Cai was shocked and bewildered by the situation. The robbers ordered him to remain silent, demanding money and valuables. They rushed into the inner room, forcibly taking Cai's newborn son from the bed, and fled. Cai was heartbroken but could do nothing but watch as the robbers disappeared into the distance. Afterwards, Cai enlisted his friend Sun Xiaowuzi to negotiate with the bandits, resulting in a ransom of 510 yuan to redeem his son. At around 10 PM the other night, Ren Yinglin, a member of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team, 1st Division, Lujiazui and Yangjing Police Stations, was patrolling the river and noticed a rowboat moored at the docks where a person was arguing with the boatman. He immediately went to investigate, and the boatman claimed that he did not know this person and that the man had suddenly come to extort 1,350 yuan from him, leading to the conflict. Officer Ren suspected that there was more to the story than met the eye, so he detained both men and brought them and the rowboat to the Lujiazui Police Station. Officer Liu questioned them, and after reviewing the confusing statements of both parties, he suspected foul play. He ordered them to be sent to the South City General Team, where Chief Xu questioned them further. The boatman confessed his name as Xu Qixian, 24 years old, originally from Yancheng, Jiangbei. On the evening of December 22 of last year, he and his friend Li Youshun (the person arrested) and Sun Haoke, Hong Bin, and Pan San, along with others, went to Nanjiazi, Yancheng to kidnap Cai Huiqing's son. Because they had no weapons, they had to buy a string of firecrackers to set off outside Cai's house as a fake show of force before rushing in. Afterwards, Cai paid 510 yuan to redeem his son. At the time, Li Youshun received 150 yuan, Sun and Hong Ke received 80 yuan, Hong Bin and Pan San each received 20 yuan, and he, Xu, only received 30 yuan. Because the situation became dangerous, he fled to Shanghai. Since then, he considered this kind of business to be an unwise strategy, so he tried to purchase a rowboat in order to make a living by transporting people safely. However, Li Youshun was greedy and demanding. Tonight, he came to extort money from him again, leading to his arrest. Interrogated, Li Youshun confessed that he was 32 years old and from Yancheng. In December of last year, he, Xu Qixian, and his friends went to Nanjiazi to kidnap Cai Huiqing's son. Later, after Xu received the ransom, he fled to Shanghai and enjoyed it all by himself. Only today did he discover Xu and joined his friends Xu Da Jinbao Zi, Xu Xiao Ya Zi, and Li Sanbao to go to Xu's boat to demand that the ransom money be divided equally. Xu was stingy and refused to give them any money, leading to a dispute that was overheard by the police. When the police arrived, Xu Da and the others took the opportunity to escape first. He, Li, was too slow to react and was arrested. Because the case involved kidnapping, an official report was prepared and sent to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation and punishment.

Xu Guoying, a Key Suspect in a Kidnapping Case, Is He a Military Officer? 173

Because He Has Already Been Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

He Claims He Should Be Subjected to Military Trial

Xu Guoying, a native of Ninghai, was arrested by the Public Concession Police for committing a major kidnapping case and was sentenced to life imprisonment by the former Provisional Court. Xu refused to accept the verdict and hired lawyer Jiang Yiping to appeal, declaring that Xu was the captain of the Detective Team of the 5th Brigade of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Force and a special agent of the Provincial Government. Since he was a military officer, he should be tried by a military court, and the ordinary court had no jurisdiction. Yesterday afternoon, Chief Judge Song and Judge Du of the High Branch Court held a hearing. Chief Judge Song ordered the police lawyer to present the organizational chart of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Force for review. Xu then confessed to his previous position, stating that he was a captain. The police lawyer then stated that when Xu was arrested, the Zhejiang Provincial Government Security Force and the Garrison Command had both sent documents requesting his transfer, but the trial judge at that time determined that the Security Force was a police agency with the authority to accept and make a judgment. Xu then appealed to the appellate court, which was also rejected. This shows that he should not be under the jurisdiction of a military agency. The nature of the Security Force is similar to that of the Public Security Bureau. Xu should belong to the police force. Therefore, the research that should be done in this case is whether Xu is a military officer or a police officer. If he is a military officer, does the High Court have the authority to hear the case? These two points are very important and will be expressed in writing. Please reschedule the hearing. Lawyer Jiang continued by stating that the Security Force was organized according to the army organization law and should be treated the same as military personnel. The court ordered a rescheduling to wait for the police lawyer to submit his written opinion before reviewing it.

Laofengxiang Jewelry Store Robbed 174

Yesterday at around 1:15 PM, four robbers speaking with a northern accent stormed into Laofengxiang Jewelry Store, owned by Shanghai gentry Wang Yiting, at 26 Zhaojia Road, Dadongmen, Nanshi. Two wore black clothing, one wore gray, and one wore blue; one wore a melon-shaped cap, and the other three wore copper-basin-style felt hats. Each carried a No. 3 wooden box pistol. Two of the robbers approached the counter, pretending to be buying gold jewelry and haggling over prices. At that time, two other robbers burst in and went straight to the security guard Zhao Jingzhong, who was on duty at the store. As the guard was about to stand up, the two robbers pulled out box pistols, pointed them at him, and confiscated his Browning pistol No. 181 (containing seven bullets) and whistle. At the same time, the two robbers standing at the counter jumped over it and quickly robbed the cash drawer of 2,871 yuan in banknotes and over 200 yuan in small coins. The robbers then fled westward through the main door with their loot. The guard, seeing that the robbers had gone far away, quickly ran to report to the 2nd Precinct of the 1st District. Director Ma was attending a bureau affairs meeting at the General Bureau when he heard the alarm and rushed back to the precinct. At that time, inspectors and dozens of officers had already gone to surround and search for the robbers, but they were nowhere to be found.

Two Punches to the Head 175

A Woman Dies as a Result

People from Guan Lane Are Very Ferocious

Zhang Yu Shi, wife of Zhang Jinsong, a paper envelope business owner from Danyang, resided at No. 48 Baoxing Fang, Zhongxing Road, Zhabei. She was 33 years old and had four children, all quite mischievous. The other day, her eldest son picked up a piece of firewood from someone in Guan Lane and brought it home. Tang Denglian, from Guan Lane, saw this and beat the child. Hearing her child's cries, Mrs. Zhang went out to reason with him, but Tang punched her twice in the head. Mrs. Zhang immediately collapsed to the ground. The police took Tang into custody at the Fourth District Police Station and sent Mrs. Zhang to Jisheng Hospital, where she died yesterday despite treatment. No More Fake Wine in the Market 176

Impressions of the Preciousness of Gold and the Cunning of Merchants

Since Li Guangzhen took charge of the Second District Baijiu Excise Office, two and a half years have passed with good results. Because over fifty wine shops in the city often sell adulterated liquor, which is harmful to hygiene, he immediately ordered all inspectors to prohibit it. The amount of liquor transported from the wine-producing areas of Hengjing in Pudong and the Jiangbei area has also gradually increased. Furthermore, since the price of gold has risen, both genuine and adulterated liquor have become expensive, so most of the adulterated liquor in the city has largely disappeared from the market.

Minutes of the Board Meeting of the Miscellaneous Grains Exchange 178

The Stock of this Exchange Reduced to 30,000 Shares

The Shanghai Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cake Exchange held a board meeting yesterday afternoon. Chairman Lai Huijun reported the purpose of the meeting and stated that the stock of the exchange had previously been 50,000 shares. For the sake of consolidating credit, the tenth shareholders' meeting resolved to reduce the stock of the exchange to 30,000 shares. With the reduction of shares, the remaining shares should be immediately redeemed. After discussion among the merchants, it was decided that all remaining shares would be redeemed at the original price of the exchange, and dividends would be paid. As all shareholders are in the same industry, a notice should be published in the newspaper, instructing all shareholders to fill out a report and submit it to the exchange to receive a temporary receipt. After one month, new shares will be exchanged for the receipt. In addition, a letter will be sent to each shareholder for notification, and it is hoped that there will be no delay.

Dr. Yuan Wenduo Sued 183

Chen Youming, a Dantu native residing at No. 15 Peng Road, sought treatment from Dr. Yuan Wenduo's clinic at No. 273 Fengtian Road on the first day of last month due to illness. After diagnosis, Yuan gave him a prescription. The prescribed medicine contained eight fen of western ephedra, four fen of asarum, and eight fen of light dried ginger. Chen was suffering from insomnia and indigestion. After taking the medicine, his symptoms suddenly changed. That night, he became feverish and lost consciousness. By morning, he was coughing up blood, and his life was in danger. He immediately went back for a follow-up visit and told Yuan about his condition. Yuan then realized that the medicine he had used was too strong and changed the prescription to a cooling medicine. Chen was afraid that such a combination of cold and hot, strong and mild treatments would not be effective and would lead to danger, so he abandoned the prescription and did not buy the medicine. Instead, he sought treatment from Dr. Zhou Jianbang. Dr. Zhou, after learning about the previously taken medicine, found that all the medicines were not appropriate for the symptoms, so he re-prescribed. Later, Chen asked Dr. Cai Yousheng and other doctors to evaluate Yuan's prescription. They all believed that the prescription was wrong. Fortunately, he changed doctors early, and his life was not sacrificed. Now that Chen's illness has been cured, he believes that the negligence of a doctor can be terrifying. If he is not punished by law, he will not learn a lesson. He hired lawyer Wang Shizong to file a criminal self-accusation with the Special District Local Court for negligent injury, requesting punishment according to Article 301, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law, in order to warn those negligent doctors who treat human life as a child's play. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Xiao opened the court to hear the case. The defendant, Yuan Wenduo, failed to appear, so the trial could not proceed. The judge ordered that the defendant be summoned again to appear in court for a rescheduled hearing.

News from Various Labor Unions

The Pharmaceutical Workers' Union convened a general membership meeting yesterday, with over 1,200 members in attendance. The presidium, consisting of Zhao Zhenhui, Fang Qingjian, and Zhang Jinlong, performed the ceremonies. The presidium reported the purpose of the meeting. A representative from the Citizen Training Association gave instructions (summary omitted). The election began, and the following nine people were elected as directors: Zhao Zhenhui, Fang Qingjian, Cai Mao Huai, Fang Qinghe, Feng Xingkang, Chen Hezhi, Liu Yongkang, Ying Jinde, and Ye Baozhong. The following four people were elected as alternate directors: Chen Yuantao, Sun Jusheng, Zhu Rongchen, and Zhang Jinlong. The following five people were elected as supervisors: Yuan Pinzhang, Ma Weixin, Hu Ruirong, Ye Zuren, and Yang Xuehui. Zhong Jiren and Yan Rongbing were elected as alternate supervisors. They were sworn in on the spot. Gu Bingyuan, a representative from the Social Affairs Bureau, gave instructions (summary omitted). Subsequently, the following matters were discussed: (1) Regarding how to deal with the capital side's application to amend the regulations, it was resolved unanimously to deny it and to request an increase of ten yuan per month for each person. If necessary, all members will act in unison, passed. (2) Regarding how to remedy the loss of more than ten days of wages due to the abolition of the lunar new and full moon days by various stores, while still reducing prices and extending working hours, and calculating wages according to the solar calendar, it was resolved to request the capital side to increase wages by one day each month according to the original wage increase, passed. (3) Regarding how to deal with the embezzlement of public funds by the union's executive director, it was resolved to permanently expel him from membership and request the higher authorities to handle the recovery of public funds, passed. (4) Regarding how to deal with Ye Fashu and Wei Rongkui's embezzlement and bribery, it was resolved that if the two can recover the membership cards and expel the certified persons from the store and expel them from membership within one month, they will be expelled from membership for three months; otherwise, they will be expelled from membership for three years, passed. (5) Regarding how to deal with Wang Youcai's introduction of fraud, it was resolved to expel him from membership for one year. If he can handle the previous case, his expulsion from membership will be reduced to two months, passed. (6) Regarding the recent dismissal of blameless workers by various stores, knowing that the situation is false and lacking reason, and often hiring lawyers to intimidate and force members to leave the store, how should we deal with it? It was resolved to notify all members that if they encounter the same situation in the future, they are not allowed to accept it, and to send a public letter to the Lawyers Association to stop members from interfering in labor disputes without authorization, passed. (7) Should the workers' association attached to the union elect administrative personnel and how many people should be elected? It was resolved to elect fifteen people and elected Fang Qingjian, Zhang Jinlong, Wang Meisheng, Fang Tingyu, Zhao Zhenhui, Tang Wenliang, Lin Jinfu, Zhang Tongfu, Li Jinsheng, Chen Hezhi, Lan Shenxiu, Wang Kaichun, Feng Xingkang, Ye Baozhong, and Shi Zongliang as administrative personnel of the association.

The meeting was adjourned with slogans and refreshments.

The Zhabei District Cotton Textile Industry Union held a representative meeting on the 14th. Over 40 representatives attended. Zhang Yufu chaired the meeting. The election resulted in Gu Yucheng, Shen Zifu, Zhang Zongyuan, Xue Pinzhang, Zhong Xiaobao, Wu Biyu, and Lu Xuezong being elected as directors, Wang Xiaomei, Shen A'da, and Yunfu as alternate directors, Zhang Yufu, Ye Jinfeng, and Zhang Ziliang as supervisors, and Song Caiyun as an alternate supervisor. Representatives from the higher level supervised the inauguration. On the 16th, a joint meeting of directors and supervisors was held. Gu Yucheng chaired the meeting. Shen Zifu and Gu Yucheng were elected as executive directors, and Zhang Yufu as executive supervisor.

The Shanghai South District Water and Electricity Industry Union held its first board meeting yesterday. Chairman Xu Yusheng performed the ceremonies. (A) Report items (omitted). (B) Election of executive directors: (1) Elected: Zhu Hancu, Zhou Guangrong, Tang Junsheng, Fang Ronggeng, and Xu Wangsheng. (2) Assignment of work: General Affairs Department - Fang Ronggeng, Organization Department - Xu Wangsheng, Propaganda Department and Accounting - Zhu Hancu, Liaison Section - Tang Junsheng, Investigation Section - Zhou Bingsheng, General Affairs Section and Document Section - Zhou Guangrong. (C) Discussion items: (1) Should the seals used by various departments within the union be changed? It was resolved to change all of them. (2) What procedures should be followed to amend the labor-capital contract? It was resolved that the union should first amend it separately with the capital side. (3) The capital side gave less double pay for the New Year. It was resolved to submit it to the Social Affairs Bureau for handling. (4) There is a lack of passenger notice signs inside the trams. It was resolved to ask the company to quickly install the equipment.

The Zhabei District Wood and Water Industry Union held its first joint meeting of directors and supervisors the day before yesterday. Chairman Wang Guoxing (acting). (A) Chairman's report. (B) Discussion items: (1) It was resolved to appoint Shao Shunqing and Zhou Chengyuan as executive directors, Tang Yingzhou as executive supervisor, Xia Yueshan as director of the guidance section, Zhu Yunqing as director of the general affairs section, Chen Lansheng as director of the investigation section, Zhao Rongqing as the head of the school affairs committee, Lu Yunzhang as the accountant and general affairs officer, Dong as the labor children's school teacher and disciplinarian, Shao Shunqing, Tang Yingzhou, Zhou Chengyuan, and Min Yuncai as the investigators. (2) It was resolved that the date of the directors' meeting will be held on the 14th and 30th of each month, and the date of the supervisors' meeting will be held on the 1st of each month. (3) It was resolved that the daily office hours are from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM and from 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM. (4) It was resolved that the old bill will be changed to the words "Wood and Water" and used as is.

The Cigarette Industry Pudong District Union held its first board meeting the night before last. Chairman Chen Peide. Discussion items: 1. Assignment of work case: The results of the election were: Executive Chen Peide, Gu Ruofeng, Liu Dehua, General Affairs Xiao Gengsheng, Organization Li Guangxian, Bao Yangzhou, Guidance Xie Peiji, Propaganda Fei Keguang, Investigation Hu Xiaomei. 2. Regulations on the system of account books: It was resolved that the accounting director should prepare a detailed statement of income and expenditure on a monthly basis. The income should be handed over to the general affairs section for safekeeping every night, and the expenses should be claimed by the general affairs section. 3. Regarding the management of membership stamps, it was resolved that the general affairs section should keep them in custody and the supervisors should review and stamp them every month and forward them to the organization section for distribution to each branch. 4. Rules for the Board meeting: It was resolved that the meeting should be convened by the General Affairs Section every Saturday afternoon.

The Seafarers Branch held its 13th standing meeting yesterday. (A) Report Items (omitted). (B) Discussion Items: (1) Jianghua Lun Zhang Guilin reported that the vacancies of Xiang Jin Erren had been filled by alternates. Resolved to convene a meeting when the ship arrives to resolve the matter. (2) Ning Shaozhong Cabin Fang Qinghe, etc., reported that Director Xiang of the Han Branch's 13th Branch requested an increase in the price of passenger tickets without clarifying his intentions. Asked for instructions. Resolved to submit it to the General Association for thorough investigation. (3) The Chinese Cabin Office submitted a report requesting that personnel be sent to supervise the re-election. Resolved to approve it for record. (4) Difficult worker Wu Junqiu requested placement. Resolved to ask the workers of the Jianguo Lun to come to the meeting to inquire and verify. (C) Provisional Motions: (1) The comprador of the Hehe Lun dismissed five tally workers without reason. Please continue to negotiate. Resolved to approve Committee Member Tang to investigate the case. (2) The comprador of the Dahua Lun requested the association to instruct the four workers. Resolved that there is no need to discuss.

The Cantonese Rong Restaurant Dim Sum Workers' Union convened a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees yesterday. Chairman Liang Yongyi performed the ceremonies. (2) Report (omitted). Discussion Items: (A) Regarding the progress of amending the labor-capital contract, it was resolved to send a letter to the Restaurant Industry Association and to hold a labor-capital representative discussion meeting at the Cantonese Business Building at 1:00 PM on the 18th to resolve everything. (B) Regarding the reorganization problem of the association as ordered, it was resolved to notify the workers again and explain in detail. (C) The workers in Taoyuan reported that the double pay for the New Year has not yet been paid by the employer. Resolved to send a letter to the employer to make up for it to avoid any problems. (D) Regarding how to handle the workers' arrears in life insurance premiums, it was resolved to notify the workers to pay them to the association as soon as possible and send personnel to collect them; otherwise, they will not be able to enjoy the right to life insurance premiums in accordance with the regulations. The meeting was then adjourned.

(B) Regarding the date of the general meeting, it was resolved to hold the meeting at the Cantonese Rong Restaurant Dim Sum Workers' Union, 41 Yifuxing, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, at 1:00 PM on March 23rd of the lunar calendar. Acknowledgment: We received the 690th issue of the Bank Weekly from the Bank Weekly yesterday. Thank you.

Weather Report:

The Xujiahui Observatory issued the following weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: The Yangtze River basin and coastal areas will be cold and clear. There will be strong northerly to northeasterly winds in the Yellow Sea and East China Sea. The weather is bad south of Japan. Also, the highest temperature in this city in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was 50.9 degrees and the lowest was 45.9 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 61.3 degrees and the lowest was 42.6 degrees.

Shanghai Market Theater News

▲ Tianyi Film has bizarre plots and twists and turns, and the Robin Case film has bizarre plots and twists and turns that have the same effect as the previous Holmes detective case. The production has been completed and will be released soon.

▲ Zhongshan Grand Theater claims that the theater will be screening Shi Shi's case The Strange Fate of One Dart and One Sword produced by Tianyi Film Company today, and the famous Shanghai comedians Wang Wuneng and Qian Wuliang will be on stage day and night to perform Shanghai dialect plays.

Medical News

▲ Wu Zhiying Pharmacy claims that since the opening of the pharmacy, the business has been growing day by day thanks to the trust of customers. Now, the business is expanded and a branch is opened at No. 609 Taoyuanfang, North Henan Road. Because of the large price reduction before, the door was like a market, and there was a situation where it was too busy to handle. Now continue to wait for half a month to extend the deadline to the 30th of this month, and no price reduction will be made after the deadline.

▲ Yuxuan's Pharmacy, West Scissors Bridge Road, Local Hall, claims that the Jiuke Tablets issued by the pharmacy have long been tested by the Central Testing Institute. The chemical test is all made of Chinese medicine. It is effective in treating coughs and eliminating phlegm. Since its sales, it has been widely praised. For example, a Mr. Hu, who lives in Jiangyin Street, has been suffering from cough for years. He developed severely in the spring. After resting at night, he was introduced by a friend to purchase and take a box of Jiuke Tablets. After taking it, the cough stopped. After taking another box, he was cured. This pharmacy does not make profits to deceive people for the benefit of patients. In addition to branch sales offices in various ports, Yitang Lane Bridge, Lixing Shipping Bureau, and Xinzha Road Changsha Road Intersection in this city, Yixing Silk Thread in the Datouhao, South City Wharf Street, Shuncheng Letter Bureau in Lilangua Street, Sanma Road News Newspaper Office, Chongqing Road Shanghai Shops, etc. are all acting as agents to facilitate patients to try to purchase nearby.

▲ Dr. Zhang Kelun, the director of the Kelun Hospital on Tibet Road, held a banquet at Chahualou the night before last to entertain the Chinese Committee Member Chu Minyi and Mr. Xing Tian. The guests were Qian Longzhang, Shao Ruxin, and other well-known figures in the medical field. The conversation was very pleasant, and they toasted each other until about 9:00 p.m. before they all dispersed in high spirits. It is reported that Chu Minyi will have to go to Beijing due to official business and has already left for Ningbo by night train last night.

Publishing News

▲ The Zhengqi Newspaper, organized by the Plum Blossom Hall, has been published to the eighty-seventh issue. The content and printing are very exquisite. The writers are all well-known figures in Shanghai. In order to wait for the subscribers of the newspaper, those who subscribe to the newspaper directly from March 1st onwards (the newspaper fee is 2 yuan and 20 cents including postage) will be given a copy of the four-foot couplet handwritten by the owner of the Plum Blossom Hall. The address of the hall is in Yuren Lane, Yunnan Road.

Marketplace News

▲ The Meimei Electric Printing Factory claims that because of the needs of various umbrella factories in Shanghai, the factory has specially hired specialized technicians, art talents, and skilled printing workers to finely print various silk fabrics. In particular, the summer national goods umbrella printing can be carefully studied in order to improve the trends. In addition, the patterns are novel, the cost is low, and the delivery is fast and on time to answer the elegance of the patrons. For contact, please send a letter to Sanduo Lane, Fangxie Road, West Gate, to our factory.
